Hey everyone,

   This is a screenshot of the Mono Documentation browser, this is on
CVS, and what you see here is a method being rendered by the
`EcmaXmlProvider'.  The EcmaXmlProvider currently supports Class summary
rendering and method rendering.  Still missing are links, properties,
events, delegates and fields (but Duncan is on the case).

   There is still a lot left to do in other areas:

	* Bundling of the ECMA XML data into a compressed file (so
	  we do not use much space, and we do not have to depend on the
	  file system layout information as it currently does).

	* Index generation.

	* Searching of the text (Am looking into reusing the Evolution
	  text indexing engine and plug it here).

   Also, the Ecma XML format misses a few bits of information, so we
might have to "augment" the existing XML in some cases, and patch it to
be .NET compatible in others. 

   I will be working on the "bundling" of the actual information with
the tree, to avoid depending on the file system layout as we do know.

   The discussion of this will continue in mono-docs-list

   All code is on CVS, module `monodoc', the browser lives in
`monodoc/browser' together with the ecma tree compiler.

   Sorry for the big font size.

Best wishes,
Miguel.



--=-QD8/HeFhIB9RtW9hgpEM
